This was the genius of director James Cameroon. <o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><br />\n</span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">Imagine this movie without this last potent scene\u2014the movie would have been just one of those.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><br />\n</span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">Nostalgia is an emotion , only a gifted few know how to exploit and manipulate. &nbsp;<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><br />\n</span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">In the book \u201c God of small things \u201c Indian author Arundhati &nbsp;Roy used reflective reminiscence , the way nostalgia uses the quantum construct. &nbsp;Her editing of the book was jumbled , with ephemeral shattered fragments of disjointed memories strewn here and there in a clever manner.&nbsp;</span><br />\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><br /></span>\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">Imagine if she had narrated the ordinary story in tunnel vison mode\u2014nobody would have cared to read it.&nbsp;&nbsp; Events were woven magically like music . <o:p></o:p></span><br />\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://3.bp.blogspot.com/_tugjD0mUn6M/TSQlIAXAqOI/AAAAAAAACkc/wCVRZ5QvinU/s1600/images.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" src=\"https://3.bp.blogspot.com/_tugjD0mUn6M/TSQlIAXAqOI/AAAAAAAACkc/wCVRZ5QvinU/s1600/images.jpg\" /></a></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><br />\n</span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">My old school is now the Indian Government telephones building. &nbsp;It was actually a rich man\u2019s house. During rains we held the school assembly in the grand master bed room. When my wife goes to pay the telephone bills, &nbsp;when I am on leave, I tag along.&nbsp; </span><br />\n<br />\nAs soon as I enter the building , the past leads me by by pineal gland, evoking a flood , nay, &nbsp;torrent of memories.<br />\n<br />\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">I explore and hang around at nooks and corners of the inner sanctums &nbsp;allowing nostalgia to overtake my senses. &nbsp;Our school had the best looking girls in town.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><br />\n</span></div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://4.bp.blogspot.com/_tugjD0mUn6M/TSQmAUAg0QI/AAAAAAAACkw/C-8E4MkDUy0/s1600/images+%25284%2529.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" height=\"265\" src=\"https://4.bp.blogspot.com/_tugjD0mUn6M/TSQmAUAg0QI/AAAAAAAACkw/C-8E4MkDUy0/s400/images+%25284%2529.jpg\" width=\"400\" /></a></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><br />\n</span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">In this age of terrorism and bombs in India, getting caught in a wrong place of this sensitive building can prove very costly for me including prosecution and loss of passport. <o:p></o:p></span><br />\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"https://4.bp.blogspot.com/-a2-yc8vCRjo/XKBUZ88sD8I/AAAAAAABgcY/PFTEJxat1QYQqVMVw6rOnG1yPpiw2xgOACLcBGAs/s1600/imddages.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" data-original-height=\"177\" data-original-width=\"284\" height=\"248\" src=\"https://4.bp.blogspot.com/-a2-yc8vCRjo/XKBUZ88sD8I/AAAAAAABgcY/PFTEJxat1QYQqVMVw6rOnG1yPpiw2xgOACLcBGAs/s400/imddages.jpg\" width=\"400\" /></a></div>\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><br />\n</span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">But then just like love, &nbsp;nostalgia makes you absolutely defenseless and vulnerable, as if you are outside the fabric of space time, behind the quantum screen. &nbsp;You are a bit silly, and will not care for the severe consequences. <o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://1.bp.blogspot.com/_tugjD0mUn6M/TSQlRy4LZTI/AAAAAAAACkk/gYKihd3RdPA/s1600/images+%25282%2529.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" height=\"320\" src=\"https://1.bp.blogspot.com/_tugjD0mUn6M/TSQlRy4LZTI/AAAAAAAACkk/gYKihd3RdPA/s320/images+%25282%2529.jpg\" width=\"320\" /></a></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><br />\n</span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">Your vigil is totally relaxed. You hardly notice how time flies. You are in the midst of a magical autobiographical quantum memory, with your subconscious calling the shots.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><br />\n</span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">Nostalgia causes interaction with deep rooted emotions and feelings within the psyche, and hence has the power. It can be a difficult emotion and trigger sadness , at it is a bitter-sweet recall of past events and old emotions .<o:p></o:p></span><br />\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"https://1.bp.blogspot.com/-pP9aZrWMdjE/XKBVJ4ZFwFI/AAAAAAABgco/je8PDZcdmz8TWX6Y63STltu8mUu1RTNwwCLcBGAs/s1600/imaeges.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" data-original-height=\"194\" data-original-width=\"259\" height=\"299\" src=\"https://1.bp.blogspot.com/-pP9aZrWMdjE/XKBVJ4ZFwFI/AAAAAAABgco/je8PDZcdmz8TWX6Y63STltu8mUu1RTNwwCLcBGAs/s400/imaeges.jpg\" width=\"400\" /></a></div>\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><br />\n</span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">Nostalgia gives you a dull pain inside the heart , as you know there is no reverse gear\u2014 paradoxically&nbsp; Utopia in reverse.&nbsp;&nbsp;</span><br />\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><br /></span>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"https://3.bp.blogspot.com/-FQmlbl5cncg/XKBUv8BxpOI/AAAAAAABgcg/VNG9VO0mD-oWr4kdHMHfXYnHPihpzhVlQCLcBGAs/s1600/idemages.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" data-original-height=\"180\" data-original-width=\"281\" height=\"256\" src=\"https://3.bp.blogspot.com/-FQmlbl5cncg/XKBUv8BxpOI/AAAAAAABgcg/VNG9VO0mD-oWr4kdHMHfXYnHPihpzhVlQCLcBGAs/s400/idemages.jpg\" width=\"400\" /></a></div>\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><br /></span>\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">Old events can never happen again.&nbsp; Old personalities can never be the same again. &nbsp;A feeling of sadness and longing is not akin to pain, and resembles sorrow only as mist resembles the rain.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><br />\n</span></div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://3.bp.blogspot.com/_tugjD0mUn6M/TSQlxFs4FsI/AAAAAAAACks/h-UIZlxbJnc/s1600/049.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" height=\"395\" src=\"https://3.bp.blogspot.com/_tugjD0mUn6M/TSQlxFs4FsI/AAAAAAAACks/h-UIZlxbJnc/s640/049.jpg\" width=\"640\" /></a></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><br />\n</span></div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n</div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><br />\n</span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">A quantum wave of presence swirls around another wave of loss, with only your consciousness collapsing it. &nbsp;This is way different from sentiments and remembrance.<o:p></o:p></span><br />\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><br />\n</span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://1.bp.blogspot.com/_tugjD0mUn6M/TSRDEJ-vrUI/AAAAAAAACk8/zF8g4W9De6o/s1600/002.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; , serif;\"><br />\n</span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">Nostalgia is a Greek word \u2013 nostos meaning home , and algos meaning pain. The literal meaning is grossly misplaced as nostalgia is home sickness only for the insensitive .<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><br />\n</span></div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://4.bp.blogspot.com/_tugjD0mUn6M/TSQlNViE1QI/AAAAAAAACkg/LfJ2YF_H6u8/s1600/download.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" height=\"266\" src=\"https://4.bp.blogspot.com/_tugjD0mUn6M/TSQlNViE1QI/AAAAAAAACkg/LfJ2YF_H6u8/s400/download.jpg\" width=\"400\" /></a></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><br />\n</span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">I love to sit amidst &nbsp;old ruins and feel the delicious pain, all the while conjuring up images of a grand past. Some magic inside the subconscious mind -- past becomes present for that fleeting moment , with emotional chords doing a sweet twang!.&nbsp; <o:p></o:p></span><br />\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><br />\n</span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://2.bp.blogspot.com/_tugjD0mUn6M/TSiiHQuNkqI/AAAAAAAACmQ/nvnIVBfpnk0/s1600/images+%252812%2529.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; , serif;\"><br />\n</span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">I do believe that this planet will wake up to the clouds of mystic nostalgia , and \u201c ruins tourism\u201d will take off in a loveless future world . &nbsp;There is no surer trigger for this bitter sweet emotion.</span><br />\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><br />\n</span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">It is healthy too , as looking backwards for a while , with respect and awe , formats the mind rendering it fitter for the present and the future.</span><br />\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot;
